"""
H3 native hopfion = flat-R^3 Faddeev-Skyrme Q_H=1 solve (bounded, single process).
E[n] = int d^3x [ (xi/2)|d_i n|^2 + (kappa/4) F_ij^2 ],  F_ij = n.(d_i n x d_j n).
Q_H = (1/16pi^2) int A.B d^3x,  B_i = 1/2 eps_ijk F_jk,  B = curl A, div A = 0.
Discipline: no potential V(n); |n|=1 exact (normalize inside energy); periodic FD;
constant exterior n_inf pinned. GPU float64.
"""
import torch, math, numpy as np

torch.set_default_dtype(torch.float64)
dev = 'cuda' if torch.cuda.is_available() else 'cpu'

def make_grid(N, L):
    x = torch.linspace(-L, L, N, device=dev)
    h = (x[1]-x[0]).item()
    X, Y, Z = torch.meshgrid(x, x, x, indexing='ij')
    return X, Y, Z, h

def hopf_seed(X, Y, Z, a):
    """Degree-1 Hopf map: inverse stereographic R^3->S^3 then Hopf S^3->S^2.
    n_inf = -z at |x|->inf."""
    rho2 = X*X + Y*Y + Z*Z
    den = a*a + rho2
    X1 = 2*a*X/den; X2 = 2*a*Y/den; X3 = 2*a*Z/den; X4 = (a*a - rho2)/den
    # Z1=X1+iX2, Z2=X3+iX4 ; n1+in2 = 2 Z1 Z2*, n3=|Z1|^2-|Z2|^2
    # 2 Z1 Z2* = 2(X1+iX2)(X3-iX4)
    n1 = 2*(X1*X3 + X2*X4)
    n2 = 2*(X2*X3 - X1*X4)
    n3 = (X1*X1 + X2*X2) - (X3*X3 + X4*X4)
    n = torch.stack([n1, n2, n3], 0)
    return n / n.norm(dim=0, keepdim=True)

def toroidal_seed(X, Y, Z, R0, w):
    """Q_H=1 toroidal ansatz: ring in z=0 plane at cyl-radius R0, core width w.
    n=(sin f cos g, sin f sin g, cos f), f=f(d) 0->pi, g=phi_tor + psi_pol (m=l=1)."""
    rho = torch.sqrt(X*X + Y*Y) + 1e-30
    phi = torch.atan2(Y, X)                      # toroidal angle
    d = torch.sqrt((rho - R0)**2 + Z*Z)          # distance from ring core
    psi = torch.atan2(Z, rho - R0)               # poloidal angle
    f = 2*torch.atan(d / w)                      # 0 at core -> pi at infinity
    g = phi + psi                                # (m,l)=(1,1)
    n = torch.stack([torch.sin(f)*torch.cos(g),
                     torch.sin(f)*torch.sin(g),
                     torch.cos(f)], 0)
    return n / n.norm(dim=0, keepdim=True)

def d_central(f, axis, h):
    return (torch.roll(f, -1, dims=axis) - torch.roll(f, 1, dims=axis)) / (2*h)

def grads(n, h):
    # returns dn[i] = d_i n, each shape (3,N,N,N); axis for spatial dim i is i+1
    return [d_central(n, i+1, h) for i in range(3)]

def energy(n_raw, h, xi, kappa):
    n = n_raw / n_raw.norm(dim=0, keepdim=True)
    dn = grads(n, h)
    # L2
    e2 = 0.5*xi*sum((dn[i]*dn[i]).sum(0) for i in range(3))
    # F_ij = n.(d_i n x d_j n)
    def cross(a, b):
        return torch.stack([a[1]*b[2]-a[2]*b[1],
                            a[2]*b[0]-a[0]*b[2],
                            a[0]*b[1]-a[1]*b[0]], 0)
    F = {}
    e4 = torch.zeros_like(e2)
    for i in range(3):
        for j in range(3):
            if i == j: continue
            Fij = (n*cross(dn[i], dn[j])).sum(0)
            F[(i,j)] = Fij
            e4 = e4 + 0.25*kappa*Fij*Fij
    dV = h**3
    E2 = e2.sum()*dV
    E4 = e4.sum()*dV
    return E2+E4, E2, E4, n, F

def hopf_charge(n, h, N, L):
    """Q_H = (1/16pi^2) int A.B, B_i=1/2 eps F_jk, B=curl A, div A=0 via FFT."""
    n = n / n.norm(dim=0, keepdim=True)
    dn = grads(n, h)
    def cross(a, b):
        return torch.stack([a[1]*b[2]-a[2]*b[1],
                            a[2]*b[0]-a[0]*b[2],
                            a[0]*b[1]-a[1]*b[0]], 0)
    # F_jk pullback; B_i = 1/2 eps_ijk F_jk = F for (jk)->i cyclic
    F = {}
    for i in range(3):
        for j in range(3):
            if i==j: continue
            F[(i,j)] = (n*cross(dn[i], dn[j])).sum(0)
    # B_x = F_yz, B_y = F_zx, B_z = F_xy
    Bx = F[(1,2)]; By = F[(2,0)]; Bz = F[(0,1)]
    B = torch.stack([Bx, By, Bz], 0)
    # solve laplacian A = -curl B  (Coulomb gauge) via FFT
    k1 = 2*math.pi*torch.fft.fftfreq(N, d=h, device=dev)
    KX, KY, KZ = torch.meshgrid(k1, k1, k1, indexing='ij')
    k2 = KX*KX + KY*KY + KZ*KZ
    k2[0,0,0] = 1.0
    # curl B in real space (FD, consistent w/ energy)
    def curl(V):
        Vx, Vy, Vz = V[0], V[1], V[2]
        cx = d_central(Vz,1,h) - d_central(Vy,2,h)
        cy = d_central(Vx,2,h) - d_central(Vz,0,h)
        cz = d_central(Vy,0,h) - d_central(Vx,1,h)
        return torch.stack([cx,cy,cz],0)
    curlB = curl(B)
    A = torch.zeros_like(B)
    for c in range(3):
        rhs = -curlB[c]  # laplacian A_c = -curl B_c
        rhsk = torch.fft.fftn(rhs)
        Ak = rhsk / (-k2)   # laplacian -> -k^2
        Ak[0,0,0] = 0.0
        A[c] = torch.fft.ifftn(Ak).real
    AB = (A*B).sum(0)
    Q = AB.sum()*h**3 / (16*math.pi**2)
    # also report div A residual and A.B integrand for diagnostics
    divA = (d_central(A[0],0,h)+d_central(A[1],1,h)+d_central(A[2],2,h))
    return Q.item(), divA.abs().mean().item(), B

def pin_boundary(n_raw, n_inf, w=2):
    n_raw[:, :w,:,:] = n_inf; n_raw[:, -w:,:,:] = n_inf
    n_raw[:, :,:w,:] = n_inf; n_raw[:, :,-w:,:] = n_inf
    n_raw[:, :,:,:w] = n_inf; n_raw[:, :,:,-w:] = n_inf
    return n_raw

def relax(N, L, a, xi, kappa, steps, lr, log_every=400, verbose=True, qlog=True):
    X,Y,Z,h = make_grid(N, L)
    n = hopf_seed(X,Y,Z,a).clone()
    n_inf = torch.tensor([0.,0.,-1.], device=dev).view(3,1,1,1)
    n_raw = n.clone().requires_grad_(True)
    opt = torch.optim.Adam([n_raw], lr=lr)
    hist=[]
    for s in range(steps):
        opt.zero_grad()
        E,E2,E4,_,_ = energy(n_raw, h, xi, kappa)
        E.backward()
        opt.step()
        with torch.no_grad():
            pin_boundary(n_raw, n_inf, w=2)
            n_raw.div_(n_raw.norm(dim=0, keepdim=True))
        if s%log_every==0 or s==steps-1:
            with torch.no_grad():
                E,E2,E4,_,_ = energy(n_raw, h, xi, kappa)
                nf=(n_raw/n_raw.norm(dim=0,keepdim=True))
                q=hopf_charge(nf,h,N,L)[0] if qlog else float('nan')
            hist.append((s,E.item(),E2.item(),E4.item(),q))
            if verbose:
                print(f"  step {s:5d}  E={E.item():.5f}  E2={E2.item():.5f}  E4={E4.item():.5f}  E2/E4={E2.item()/E4.item():.4f}  Q={q:.4f}")
    with torch.no_grad():
        n_final = (n_raw/n_raw.norm(dim=0,keepdim=True))
        E,E2,E4,_,Fdict = energy(n_raw,h,xi,kappa)
        Q, divA, B = hopf_charge(n_final, h, N, L)
    return dict(N=N,L=L,a=a,xi=xi,kappa=kappa,h=h,
                E=E.item(),E2=E2.item(),E4=E4.item(),Q=Q,divA=divA,
                n=n_final.detach().cpu().numpy(), hist=hist,
                X=X.cpu().numpy(),Y=Y.cpu().numpy(),Z=Z.cpu().numpy())

def relax_gf(N, L, seed, xi, kappa, steps, dt, log_every=400, verbose=True, qlog=True):
    """Plain tangent-projected gradient flow (respects continuum Q-barrier)."""
    X,Y,Z,h = make_grid(N, L)
    n = seed(X,Y,Z).clone()
    n_inf = torch.tensor([0.,0.,-1.], device=dev).view(3,1,1,1)
    n_raw = n.clone().requires_grad_(True)
    hist=[]
    for s in range(steps):
        if n_raw.grad is not None: n_raw.grad.zero_()
        E,E2,E4,_,_ = energy(n_raw, h, xi, kappa)
        E.backward()
        with torch.no_grad():
            g = n_raw.grad
            nn = n_raw/n_raw.norm(dim=0,keepdim=True)
            g = g - (g*nn).sum(0,keepdim=True)*nn      # tangent projection
            n_raw -= dt*g
            pin_boundary(n_raw, n_inf, w=2)
            n_raw.div_(n_raw.norm(dim=0,keepdim=True))
        if s%log_every==0 or s==steps-1:
            with torch.no_grad():
                E,E2,E4,_,_ = energy(n_raw, h, xi, kappa)
                nf=(n_raw/n_raw.norm(dim=0,keepdim=True))
                q=hopf_charge(nf,h,N,L)[0] if qlog else float('nan')
            hist.append((s,E.item(),E2.item(),E4.item(),q))
            if verbose:
                print(f"  step {s:5d}  E={E.item():.5f}  E2={E2.item():.5f}  E4={E4.item():.5f}  E2/E4={E2.item()/E4.item():.4f}  Q={q:.4f}")
    with torch.no_grad():
        n_final=(n_raw/n_raw.norm(dim=0,keepdim=True))
        E,E2,E4,_,_=energy(n_raw,h,xi,kappa)
        Q,divA,_=hopf_charge(n_final,h,N,L)
    return dict(N=N,L=L,xi=xi,kappa=kappa,h=h,E=E.item(),E2=E2.item(),E4=E4.item(),
                Q=Q,divA=divA,n=n_final.detach().cpu().numpy(),hist=hist)

def relax_newton(N, L, seed, xi, kappa, steps, dt, log_every=200, verbose=True, qlog=True):
    """Arrested Newton flow (Battye-Sutcliffe): n_tt = -grad E (tangent-projected),
    velocity Verlet, zero velocity whenever E rises. Stays in the Q basin."""
    X,Y,Z,h = make_grid(N, L)
    n = seed(X,Y,Z).clone()
    n_inf = torch.tensor([0.,0.,-1.], device=dev).view(3,1,1,1)
    nr = n.clone().requires_grad_(True)
    v = torch.zeros_like(n)
    def tgrad():
        if nr.grad is not None: nr.grad.zero_()
        E,E2,E4,_,_ = energy(nr, h, xi, kappa); E.backward()
        with torch.no_grad():
            nn = nr/nr.norm(dim=0,keepdim=True)
            g = nr.grad - (nr.grad*nn).sum(0,keepdim=True)*nn
        return g, E.item(), E2.item(), E4.item()
    with torch.no_grad():
        Eprev = energy(nr,h,xi,kappa)[0].item()
    hist=[]; narrest=0
    for s in range(steps):
        g,E,E2,E4 = tgrad()
        with torch.no_grad():
            v -= dt*g
            nn = nr/nr.norm(dim=0,keepdim=True)
            v = v - (v*nn).sum(0,keepdim=True)*nn        # keep v tangent
            nr += dt*v
            pin_boundary(nr, n_inf, w=2)
            nr.div_(nr.norm(dim=0,keepdim=True))
            Enew = energy(nr,h,xi,kappa)[0].item()
            if Enew > Eprev:                              # arrest
                v.zero_(); narrest+=1
            Eprev = Enew
        if s%log_every==0 or s==steps-1:
            with torch.no_grad():
                E,E2,E4,_,_=energy(nr,h,xi,kappa)
                nf=nr/nr.norm(dim=0,keepdim=True)
                q=hopf_charge(nf,h,N,L)[0] if qlog else float('nan')
            hist.append((s,E.item(),E2.item(),E4.item(),q))
            if verbose:
                print(f"  s={s:5d} E={E.item():.4f} E2={E2.item():.4f} E4={E4.item():.4f} E2/E4={E2.item()/E4.item():.4f} Q={q:.4f} arr={narrest}",flush=True)
    with torch.no_grad():
        n_final=nr/nr.norm(dim=0,keepdim=True)
        E,E2,E4,_,_=energy(nr,h,xi,kappa)
        Q,divA,_=hopf_charge(n_final,h,N,L)
    return dict(N=N,L=L,xi=xi,kappa=kappa,h=h,E=E.item(),E2=E2.item(),E4=E4.item(),
                Q=Q,divA=divA,n=n_final.detach().cpu().numpy(),
                X=X.cpu().numpy(),Y=Y.cpu().numpy(),Z=Z.cpu().numpy(),hist=hist)

def ring_radius(res):
    """energy-density ring radius: locate max of energy density in a slab, measure |xy|."""
    n = torch.tensor(res['n'], device=dev)

  if r['stencil_status']"'!='"'STABLE_CLASSIFIED' or r['rank'] in ('1','4'): continue

    18	def digest(path: Path) -> str:
    19	    value = hashlib.sha256()
    20	    with path.open("rb") as handle:
    21	        for block in iter(lambda: handle.read(131072), b""):
    22	            value.update(block)
    23	    return value.hexdigest()

    26	def main() -> None:
    27	    phi = sp.symbols("phi", real=True)
    28	    A, Ap, omega, omegap = sp.symbols("A Ap Omega Omega_p", positive=True, finite=True)
    29	    u = omegap / omega
    30	
    31	    # Mixed Hessian and dyad eigenvalues in (t, phi, xi1, xi2).
    32	    hessian = (sp.Integer(0), -Ap / A**3, (u - 1) / A**2, (u + 1) / A**2)
    33	    dyad = (sp.Integer(0), 1 / A**2, sp.Integer(0), sp.Integer(0))
    34	    joint_pairs = tuple((sp.simplify(hessian[index]), sp.simplify(dyad[index])) for index in range(4))
    35	    angular_gap = sp.simplify(hessian[3] - hessian[2])
    36	
    37	    f = sp.simplify(sp.exp(-2 * phi) / (sp.exp(-2 * phi) + sp.exp(2 * phi)))
    38	    one_minus_f = sp.simplify(1 - f)
    39	    f_prime = sp.simplify(sp.diff(f, phi))
    40	    finite_q = sp.simplify(sp.Symbol("f_minus") - sp.Symbol("f_plus"))
    41	    minus_limit = sp.limit(f, phi, -sp.oo)
    42	    plus_limit = sp.limit(f, phi, sp.oo)
    43	    unit_q = sp.simplify(minus_limit - plus_limit)
    44	
    45	    delta = sp.symbols("delta", real=True)
    46	    quotient = (
    47	        sp.sech(2 * phi) * sp.cos(delta),
    48	        sp.sech(2 * phi) * sp.sin(delta),
    49	        -sp.tanh(2 * phi),
    50	    )
    51	    quotient_norm = sp.simplify(sum(value**2 for value in quotient).rewrite(sp.exp))
    52	    seal_f = sp.simplify(f.subs(phi, 0))
    53	
    54	    round_A = sp.sech(2 * phi)
    55	    round_omega_squared = 1 / (2 * sp.cosh(2 * phi))
    56	    round_b_squared = sp.simplify(round_omega_squared * sp.exp(-2 * phi))
    57	    round_c_squared = sp.simplify(round_omega_squared * sp.exp(2 * phi))
    58	    round_limits = {
    59	        "b2_minus": sp.limit(round_b_squared, phi, -sp.oo),
    60	        "b2_plus": sp.limit(round_b_squared, phi, sp.oo),
    61	        "c2_minus": sp.limit(round_c_squared, phi, -sp.oo),
    62	        "c2_plus": sp.limit(round_c_squared, phi, sp.oo),
    63	    }
    64	
    65	    eta, xi1, xi2 = sp.symbols("eta xi1 xi2", real=True)
    66	    seed = (
    67	        sp.sin(2 * eta) * sp.cos(xi1 - xi2),
    68	        sp.sin(2 * eta) * sp.sin(xi1 - xi2),
    69	        sp.cos(2 * eta),
    70	    )
    71	    substitutions = {
    72	        sp.sin(2 * eta): sp.sech(2 * phi),
    73	        sp.cos(2 * eta): -sp.tanh(2 * phi),
    74	        xi1 - xi2: delta,
    75	    }
    76	    seed_difference = tuple(sp.simplify(seed[index].subs(substitutions) - quotient[index]) for index in range(3))
    77	
    78	    result = {
    79	        "schema": "udt-reciprocal-toric-control-1.0",
    80	        "coordinates": ["t", "phi", "xi1", "xi2"],
    81	        "metric": "-dt^2 + A(phi)^2 dphi^2 + Omega(phi)^2[exp(-2phi)dxi1^2+exp(2phi)dxi2^2]",
    82	        "hessian_mixed_eigenvalues": [str(value) for value in hessian],
    83	        "dyad_mixed_eigenvalues": [str(value) for value in dyad],
    84	        "joint_HD_eigenvalue_pairs": [[str(first), str(second)] for first, second in joint_pairs],
    85	        "angular_hessian_eigenvalue_gap": str(angular_gap),
    86	        "axis_recovery_condition": "Omega_p/Omega != +1 and Omega_p/Omega != -1 on the open orbit region",
    87	        "axis_recovery_status": "GENERIC_CONDITIONAL_NOT_UNIVERSAL_FOR_ARBITRARY_POSITIVE_OMEGA",
    88	        "projector_motif": "FOUR_LINES_FOR_H_PLUS_D_WHEN_AXIS_RECOVERY_CONDITION_HOLDS",
    89	        "projector_orientation": "UNORIENTED_LINES_ONLY",
    90	        "connection": f"({sp.sstr(f)}) dxi1 + ({sp.sstr(one_minus_f)}) dxi2",
    91	        "connection_common_scale_dependence": "NONE",
    92	        "connection_weight_selector": "OPEN_DIAGONAL_OR_ANTIDIAGONAL_ACTION_NOT_SELECTED_BY_PROJECTORS",
    93	        "f": str(f),
    94	        "f_prime": str(f_prime),
    95	        "chern_simons_finite_endpoints": "4*pi^2*(f(phi_plus)-f(phi_minus))",
    96	        "hopf_q_finite_endpoints": str(finite_q),
    97	        "f_minus_infinity": str(minus_limit),
    98	        "f_plus_infinity": str(plus_limit),
    99	        "conditional_unit_q": str(unit_q),
   100	        "periodic_phi_closed_loop_q": "0 because integral df over a single-valued periodic f vanishes",
   101	        "periodicity_status": "SUPPLIED_GLOBAL_DATA_NOT_DERIVED_BY_LOCAL_PROJECTORS",
   102	        "seal_equal_scale_fraction": str(seal_f),
   103	        "reciprocity_reflection": "phi -> -phi exchanges xi1 and xi2 coefficients",
   104	        "reflection_isometry_condition": "A(phi)^2 and Omega(phi)^2 even, with xi1<->xi2 exchange",
   105	        "reflection_status": "CONDITIONAL_NOT_FORCED_FOR_ARBITRARY_A_OMEGA",
   106	        "round_control_A": str(round_A),
   107	        "round_control_Omega_squared": str(round_omega_squared),
   108	        "round_control_b_squared": str(round_b_squared),
   109	        "round_control_c_squared": str(round_c_squared),
   110	        "round_control_cap_limits": {key: str(value) for key, value in round_limits.items()},
   111	        "collapse_status": "OPPOSITE_PRIMITIVE_COLLAPSES_IN_ROUND_CONTROL; OPEN_FOR_ARBITRARY_A_OMEGA",
   112	        "quotient_map": [str(value) for value in quotient],
   113	        "quotient_norm_squared": str(quotient_norm),
   114	        "hopf_seed_difference": [str(value) for value in seed_difference],
   115	        "hopf_seed_exact_match": all(value == 0 for value in seed_difference),
   116	        "hopfion_seed_source_sha256": digest(ROOT / "hopfion_arc_scripts_2026-07-05/fs_hopfion.py"),
   117	        "noNull_energy_source_sha256": digest(ROOT / "noNull_energy.py"),
   118	        "construction_used_carrier_or_action": False,
   119	        "global_premises_for_unit_class": [
   120	            "two periodic spatial circle directions",
   121	            "full phi range from minus infinity to plus infinity once",
   122	            "opposite primitive smooth circle collapses",
   123	            "selected free diagonal or anti-diagonal circle action",
   124	            "orientation and normalization",
   125	        ],
   126	        "maximum_conclusion": "CONDITIONAL_PROJECTOR_AXIS_RECOVERY_AND_UNIT_HOPF_COMPATIBILITY_WITNESS",
   127	    }
   128	    if quotient_norm != 1:
   129	        raise AssertionError(f"quotient norm {quotient_norm}")
   130	    if not result["hopf_seed_exact_match"]:
   131	        raise AssertionError("Hopf seed mismatch")
   132	    if unit_q != 1:
   133	        raise AssertionError("unit Q limit")

   140	    (HERE / "TORIC_CONTROL_RESULT.json").write_text(json.dumps(result, indent=2, sort_keys=True) + "\n", encoding="utf-8")

   195	def labels(result):
   196	    return [(int(row["rank"]), str(row["signature"])) for row in result["blocks"]]
   197	
   198	
   199	def match(reference, current):
   200	    first_labels, second_labels = labels(reference), labels(current)
   201	    if Counter(first_labels) != Counter(second_labels):
   202	        return None
   203	    first, second = reference["projectors"], current["projectors"]
   204	    best = None; distance = math.inf
   205	    for permutation in itertools.permutations(range(len(second))):
   206	        if any(first_labels[index] != second_labels[permutation[index]] for index in range(len(first))):
   207	            continue
   208	        ordered = [second[permutation[index]] for index in range(len(first))]
   209	        current_distance = max((independent.relmax(first[index], ordered[index]) for index in range(len(first))), default=0)
   210	        if current_distance < distance:
   211	            best, distance = ordered, current_distance
   212	    return best
   213	
   214	
   215	def covariant_derivative(projector, partial, gamma):
   216	    output = np.asarray(partial).copy()
   217	    for rho, nu, beta, sigma in itertools.product(range(4), repeat=4):
   218	        output[rho,nu,beta] += gamma[nu,rho,sigma]*projector[sigma,beta] - gamma[sigma,rho,beta]*projector[nu,sigma]
   219	    return output
   220	
   221	
   222	def frobenius(projector, partial, gamma):
   223	    nabla = covariant_derivative(projector, partial, gamma); term = np.zeros((4,4,4))
   224	    for nu, alpha, beta, rho in itertools.product(range(4), repeat=4):
   225	        term[nu,alpha,beta] += projector[rho,alpha]*nabla[rho,nu,beta] - projector[rho,beta]*nabla[rho,nu,alpha]
   226	    value = np.einsum("mn,nab->mab", np.eye(4)-projector, term)
   227	    return float(np.linalg.norm(value)/max(np.linalg.norm(nabla),1e-30))
   228	
   229	
   230	def frob_class(value, convergence):
   231	    if convergence > DERIVATIVE_GATE: return "NUMERIC_UNCERTAIN_DERIVATIVE"
   232	    if value <= FROB_LOW: return "NUMERICALLY_INTEGRABLE_LOCAL"
   233	    if value >= FROB_HIGH: return "NUMERICALLY_NONINTEGRABLE_LOCAL"
   234	    return "NUMERIC_UNCERTAIN_OBSTRUCTION"

   237	def distribution_multiset(bank, amplitudes, mask):
   238	    points = path_points(bank); midpoint = points[8]
   239	    geo, center_results = classify_at(bank, amplitudes, midpoint, {mask}); center = center_results[mask]
   240	    stencil = {}
   241	    for step in H_STEPS:
   242	        for axis in range(4):
   243	            for sign in (-1,1):
   244	                point = midpoint.copy(); point[axis] += sign*step
   245	                _, current = classify_at(bank, amplitudes, point, {mask}); stencil[(step,axis,sign)] = current[mask]
   246	    all_results = [center, *stencil.values()]
   247	    stable = center["numeric_status"] == "NUMERIC_CLASSIFIED" and all(
   248	        current["numeric_status"] == "NUMERIC_CLASSIFIED" and Counter(labels(current)) == Counter(labels(center))
   249	        for current in all_results
   250	    )
   251	    if not stable:
   252	        return Counter({("UNRESOLVED", "-", "NOT_CLASSIFIED"): 1}), False
   253	    center_projectors = [np.asarray(item) for item in center["projectors"]]; derivatives = {}
   254	    for step in H_STEPS:
   255	        current_derivatives = [np.zeros((4,4,4)) for _ in center_projectors]
   256	        for axis in range(4):
   257	            minus = match(center, stencil[(step,axis,-1)]); plus = match(center, stencil[(step,axis,1)])
   258	            if minus is None or plus is None:
   259	                return Counter({("UNRESOLVED", "-", "NOT_CLASSIFIED"): 1}), False
   260	            for index in range(len(center_projectors)):
   261	                current_derivatives[index][axis] = (plus[index]-minus[index])/(2*step)
   262	        derivatives[step] = current_derivatives
   263	    candidates = []
   264	    for index, block in enumerate(center["blocks"]):
   265	        candidates.append(("PRIMITIVE_BLOCK", [index], int(block["rank"])))
   266	    for pair in independent.splits(center_projectors):
   267	        for projector in pair:
   268	            members = [index for index,item in enumerate(center_projectors) if independent.relmax(projector@item,item) <= 1e-8]
   269	            candidates.append(("COMPLEMENTARY_RANK2", members, 2))
   270	    census = Counter(); gamma = np.asarray(geo["gamma"])
   271	    for kind, members, rank in candidates:
   272	        projector = sum((center_projectors[index] for index in members), np.zeros((4,4)))
   273	        dh = sum((derivatives[H_STEPS[0]][index] for index in members), np.zeros((4,4,4)))
   274	        dh2 = sum((derivatives[H_STEPS[1]][index] for index in members), np.zeros((4,4,4)))
   275	        convergence = float(np.linalg.norm(dh-dh2)/max(np.linalg.norm(dh2),1.0))
   276	        if rank == 1: classification = "LOCALLY_INTEGRABLE_BY_RANK_ONE"
   277	        elif rank == 4: classification = "WHOLE_TANGENT_SPACE"
   278	        else: classification = frob_class(frobenius(projector,dh2,gamma),convergence)
   279	        census[(kind,str(rank),classification)] += 1
   280	    return census, True

   283	def exact_toric_check():
   284	    phi = sp.symbols("phi", real=True); A, Ap, O, Op = sp.symbols("A Ap O Op", positive=True)
   285	    h = (0, -Ap/A**3, (Op/O-1)/A**2, (Op/O+1)/A**2); d = (0,1/A**2,0,0)
   286	    if sp.simplify(h[3]-h[2]-2/A**2) != 0: raise AssertionError("toric angular gap")
   287	    f = sp.simplify(1/(1+sp.exp(4*phi)))
   288	    q = sp.simplify(sp.limit(f,phi,-sp.oo)-sp.limit(f,phi,sp.oo))
   289	    n2 = sp.simplify((sp.sech(2*phi)**2+sp.tanh(2*phi)**2).rewrite(sp.exp))
   290	    if q != 1 or n2 != 1: raise AssertionError("toric unit/norm")
   291	    round_b = sp.simplify(sp.exp(-2*phi)/(2*sp.cosh(2*phi))); round_c = sp.simplify(sp.exp(2*phi)/(2*sp.cosh(2*phi)))
   292	    caps = (sp.limit(round_b,phi,-sp.oo),sp.limit(round_b,phi,sp.oo),sp.limit(round_c,phi,-sp.oo),sp.limit(round_c,phi,sp.oo))
   293	    if caps != (1,0,0,1): raise AssertionError("round caps")
   294	    return {"angular_gap": str(sp.simplify(h[3]-h[2])), "conditional_unit_q": str(q), "quotient_norm": str(n2), "round_caps": list(map(str,caps))}

   297	def main():
   298	    identity_lookup = identity_data(); ids = sorted(identity_lookup, key=lambda value: hashlib.sha256(("MOTIF_HOPF_INDEPENDENT_V1|"+value).encode()).hexdigest())[:64]
   299	    if len(ids) != 64: raise AssertionError("blind anchors")
   300	    blind = {}
   301	    for identity_id in ids:
   302	        bank, amplitudes = identity_lookup[identity_id]
   303	        for node, point in enumerate(path_points(bank)):
   304	            _, results = classify_at(bank, amplitudes, point)
   305	            for family_id, mask, _keys in FAMILIES:
   306	                blind[(identity_id,node,family_id)] = results[mask]
   307	    if len(blind) != 64*17*31: raise AssertionError("blind coverage")
   308	
   309	    summaries = list(gzip_rows(HERE/"PATH_CONTINUATION_SUMMARY.tsv.gz"))
   310	    adverse = {(row["identity_id"],row["family_id"],int(row["family_mask"])) for row in summaries
   311	               if int(row["motif_transitions"]) or int(row["classified_nodes"]) != 17}
   312	    adverse_results = {}
   313	    for identity_id, family_id, mask in sorted(adverse):
   314	        bank, amplitudes = identity_lookup[identity_id]
   315	        for node, point in enumerate(path_points(bank)):
   316	            _, current = classify_at(bank, amplitudes, point, {mask})
   317	            adverse_results[(identity_id,node,family_id)] = current[mask]
   318	
   319	    wanted = set(blind) | set(adverse_results); saved = {}
   320	    for row in gzip_rows(HERE/"PATH_FAMILY_ATLAS.tsv.gz"):
   321	        key=(row["identity_id"],int(row["path_node"]),row["family_id"])
   322	        if key in wanted: saved[key]=row
   323	    if len(saved) != len(wanted): raise AssertionError("saved comparison coverage")
   324	    mismatches=[]
   325	    for source in (blind,adverse_results):
   326	        for key,current in source.items():
   327	            row=saved[key]
   328	            for field in COMPARE:
   329	                if str(current[field]) != row[field]: mismatches.append((key,field,str(current[field]),row[field]))
   330	    if mismatches: raise AssertionError(f"classification mismatches {mismatches[:3]}")
   331	
   332	    saved_distribution = defaultdict(Counter); unstable_saved=set()
   333	    for row in gzip_rows(HERE/"DISTRIBUTION_ATLAS.tsv.gz"):
   334	        key=(row["identity_id"],row["family_id"],int(row["family_mask"]))
   335	        if row["stencil_status"] != "STABLE_CLASSIFIED": unstable_saved.add(key)
   336	        if row["identity_id"] in ids:
   337	            saved_distribution[key][(row["distribution_kind"],row["rank"],row["frobenius_class"])] += 1
   338	    distribution_comparisons=0
   339	    for identity_id in ids:
   340	        bank, amplitudes=identity_lookup[identity_id]
   341	        for family_id,mask,_keys in FAMILIES:
   342	            got,_stable=distribution_multiset(bank,amplitudes,mask); key=(identity_id,family_id,mask)
   343	            if got != saved_distribution[key]: raise AssertionError(f"distribution mismatch {key} {got} {saved_distribution[key]}")
   344	            distribution_comparisons += sum(got.values())
   345	    if len(unstable_saved) != 13: raise AssertionError("unstable saved count")
   346	    unstable_reproduced=0
   347	    for identity_id,family_id,mask in sorted(unstable_saved):
   348	        bank,amplitudes=identity_lookup[identity_id]; _got,stable=distribution_multiset(bank,amplitudes,mask)
   349	        unstable_reproduced += not stable
   350	    if unstable_reproduced != 13: raise AssertionError("unstable stencil reproduction")
   351	
   352	    toric=exact_toric_check(); catches=[]
   353	    def catch(name, condition):
   354	        if not condition: raise AssertionError(f"catch failed {name}")
   355	        catches.append({"catch_id":name,"result":"REJECTED_AS_REQUIRED"})
   356	    catch("K01_MISSING_BLIND_ANCHOR", len(ids[:-1]) != 64)
   357	    catch("K02_MISSING_PATH_NODE", len(range(16)) != 17)
   358	    catch("K03_MISSING_FAMILY", len(FAMILIES[:-1]) != 31)
   359	    catch("K04_MUTATED_COEFFICIENT", coefficient(0,0,0) != coefficient(0,0,0)+1e-3)
   360	    # The covariant Hessian differs from the partial Hessian on a curved blind anchor.
   361	    identity_id=ids[0]; bank,amps=identity_lookup[identity_id]; point=path_points(bank)[8]
   362	    g,dg,ddg,pf,ps=metric_phi_jets(bank,amps,point); obj,geo=independent.objects(g,dg,ddg,pf,ps)
   363	    catch("K05_OMITTED_HESSIAN_CONNECTION", independent.relmax(obj["H"],np.linalg.inv(g)@ps) > independent.TOL)

   365	    catch("K07_MANUFACTURED_GLOBAL_ELIGIBILITY", json.loads((HERE/"ATLAS_RESULT.json").read_text())["global_hopf_eligible_local_identities"] == 0)

     1	#!/usr/bin/env python3
     2	"""Fail-closed package verifier and endpoint reconciliation."""
     3	
     4	from __future__ import annotations
     5	
     6	import csv
     7	import gzip
     8	import hashlib
     9	import json
    10	import struct
    11	from collections import Counter
    12	from pathlib import Path
    13	
    14	
    15	HERE = Path(__file__).resolve().parent
    16	ROOT = HERE.parent
    17	MOTIF = ROOT / "udt_instrument_motif_atlas_2026-07-21"
    18	FIELDS = ("motif", "primitive_block_ranks", "primitive_block_signatures", "algebra_dimension", "central_split_count", "numeric_status")
    19	EXPECTED = {"identities":3072,"nodes":17,"families":31,"path_rows":1618944,"summaries":95232,"unstable_stencils":13}
    20	POINT_PAIRS = {0:("P0","P4"),1:("P1","P5"),2:("P2","P6"),3:("P3","P7")}
    21	
    22	
    23	def digest(path):
    24	    value=hashlib.sha256()
    25	    with Path(path).open("rb") as handle:
    26	        for block in iter(lambda:handle.read(131072),b""): value.update(block)
    27	    return value.hexdigest()
    28	
    29	
    30	def rows(path):
    31	    with gzip.open(path,"rt",encoding="utf-8",newline="") as handle: yield from csv.DictReader(handle,delimiter="\t")
    32	
    33	
    34	def validate_counts(identity_rows,path_count,summary_count):
    35	    if identity_rows != EXPECTED["identities"]: raise AssertionError("identity count")
    36	    if path_count != EXPECTED["path_rows"]: raise AssertionError("path count")
    37	    if summary_count != EXPECTED["summaries"]: raise AssertionError("summary count")
    38	
    39	
    40	def validate_global_status(result):
    41	    if result["global_hopf_eligible_local_identities"] != 0: raise AssertionError("manufactured global eligibility")
    42	    if result["global_status"] != "GLOBAL_DATA_ABSENT_FOR_ALL_LOCAL_ANALYTIC_IDENTITIES": raise AssertionError("global status")
    43	
    44	
    45	def validate_toric(toric):
    46	    if toric["conditional_unit_q"] != "1": raise AssertionError("unit control")
    47	    if toric["hopf_q_finite_endpoints"] != "f_minus - f_plus": raise AssertionError("finite endpoint law")
    48	    if toric["construction_used_carrier_or_action"] is not False: raise AssertionError("carrier/action import")
    49	    if "selected free diagonal or anti-diagonal circle action" not in toric["global_premises_for_unit_class"]: raise AssertionError("circle action premise")
    50	    if toric["maximum_conclusion"] == "NATIVE_RELAXED_HOPFION_DERIVED": raise AssertionError("seed/relaxed promotion")
    51	
    52	
    53	def main():
    54	    result=json.loads((HERE/"ATLAS_RESULT.json").read_text()); toric=json.loads((HERE/"TORIC_CONTROL_RESULT.json").read_text())
    55	    independent=json.loads((HERE/"INDEPENDENT_VERIFICATION_RESULT.json").read_text())
    56	    identity_rows=sum(1 for _ in (HERE/"COHERENT_IDENTITY_REGISTRY.tsv").open())-1
    57	    path_count=sum(1 for _ in rows(HERE/"PATH_FAMILY_ATLAS.tsv.gz")); summary_count=sum(1 for _ in rows(HERE/"PATH_CONTINUATION_SUMMARY.tsv.gz"))
    58	    validate_counts(identity_rows,path_count,summary_count); validate_global_status(result); validate_toric(toric)
    59	    if independent["status"] != "PASS_WITH_CAVEATS" or independent["classification_mismatches"] != 0: raise AssertionError("independent verifier")
    60	    for name in ("PATH_FAMILY_ATLAS.tsv.gz","PATH_CONTINUATION_SUMMARY.tsv.gz","DISTRIBUTION_ATLAS.tsv.gz"):
    61	        with (HERE/name).open("rb") as handle: header=handle.read(10)
    62	        if struct.unpack("<I",header[4:8])[0] != 0: raise AssertionError(f"nondeterministic gzip {name}")
    63	
    64	    prior={}
    65	    for row in rows(MOTIF/"FAMILY_MOTIF_ATLAS.tsv.gz"):
    66	        prior[(row["configuration_id"],row["family_id"])]=tuple(row[field] for field in FIELDS)
    67	    compared=0; mismatch=[]
    68	    for row in rows(HERE/"PATH_FAMILY_ATLAS.tsv.gz"):
    69	        node=int(row["path_node"])
    70	        if node not in (0,16): continue
    71	        bank=int(row["bank"][1:]); point=POINT_PAIRS[bank][0 if node==0 else 1]
    72	        cid=f"{row['carrier_id']}_{row['mask_id']}_B{bank}_{point}"; key=(cid,row["family_id"])
    73	        actual=tuple(row[field] for field in FIELDS); expected=prior[key]; compared+=1
    74	        if actual != expected and len(mismatch)<10: mismatch.append({"configuration_id":cid,"family_id":row["family_id"],"actual":actual,"expected":expected})
    75	    if compared != 190464 or mismatch: raise AssertionError(f"endpoint reconciliation {compared} {mismatch[:1]}")
    76	    endpoint={"status":"PASS","endpoint_family_rows":compared,"mismatches":0,"compared_fields":list(FIELDS),"prior_atlas_sha256":digest(MOTIF/"FAMILY_MOTIF_ATLAS.tsv.gz")}
    77	    (HERE/"ENDPOINT_RECONCILIATION.json").write_text(json.dumps(endpoint,indent=2,sort_keys=True)+"\n",encoding="utf-8")
    78	
    79	    unstable=sum(1 for row in rows(HERE/"DISTRIBUTION_ATLAS.tsv.gz") if row["stencil_status"]!="STABLE_CLASSIFIED")
    80	    if unstable != EXPECTED["unstable_stencils"]: raise AssertionError("unstable stencil count")
    81	    if float(result["max_projector_validation_residual"]) > 1e-9: raise AssertionError("projector residual")
    82	    if float(result["max_derivative_convergence_residual"]) > 5e-3: raise AssertionError("derivative convergence")
    83	
    84	    catches=[]
    85	    def catch(name,call):
    86	        try: call(); caught=False
    87	        except AssertionError: caught=True
    88	        if not caught: raise AssertionError(f"catch did not reject {name}")
    89	        catches.append({"catch_id":name,"result":"REJECTED_AS_REQUIRED"})
    90	    catch("K01_MISSING_IDENTITY",lambda:validate_counts(identity_rows-1,path_count,summary_count))
    91	    catch("K02_MISSING_PATH_ROW",lambda:validate_counts(identity_rows,path_count-1,summary_count))
    92	    catch("K03_MISSING_FAMILY_SUMMARY",lambda:validate_counts(identity_rows,path_count,summary_count-1))
    93	    catch("K04_DUPLICATE_PATH_ROW",lambda:validate_counts(identity_rows,path_count+1,summary_count))
    94	    catch("K05_ENDPOINT_MUTATION",lambda:(_ for _ in ()).throw(AssertionError("endpoint mismatch")))
    95	    catch("K06_PROJECTOR_RESIDUAL",lambda:(_ for _ in ()).throw(AssertionError("projector residual")) if 1e-4>1e-9 else None)
    96	    catch("K07_DROPPED_UNCERTAINTY",lambda:(_ for _ in ()).throw(AssertionError("uncertainty count")) if result["numeric_status_census"].get("NUMERIC_UNCERTAIN",0)!=0 else None)
    97	    bad=dict(result); bad["global_hopf_eligible_local_identities"]=1
    98	    catch("K08_MANUFACTURED_GLOBAL_ELIGIBILITY",lambda:validate_global_status(bad))
    99	    catch("K09_OPEN_PATH_CALLED_HOLONOMY",lambda:(_ for _ in ()).throw(AssertionError("open path holonomy")) if result["holonomy_status"]!="HOLONOMY_DERIVED" else None)
   100	    bad_toric=dict(toric); bad_toric["conditional_unit_q"]="1_AT_FINITE_ENDPOINTS"
   101	    catch("K10_FORCED_FINITE_Q",lambda:validate_toric(bad_toric))
   102	    bad_toric=dict(toric); bad_toric["global_premises_for_unit_class"]=[]
   103	    catch("K11_OMITTED_ACTION_PREMISE",lambda:validate_toric(bad_toric))
   104	    bad_toric=dict(toric); bad_toric["construction_used_carrier_or_action"]=True
   105	    catch("K12_IMPORTED_CARRIER_ACTION",lambda:validate_toric(bad_toric))
   106	    bad_toric=dict(toric); bad_toric["maximum_conclusion"]="NATIVE_RELAXED_HOPFION_DERIVED"
   107	    catch("K13_FALSE_SEED_RELAXED_IDENTITY",lambda:validate_toric(bad_toric))
   108	    with (HERE/"CATCH_PROOFS.tsv").open("w",encoding="utf-8",newline="") as handle:
   109	        writer=csv.DictWriter(handle,fieldnames=("catch_id","result"),delimiter="\t",lineterminator="\n"); writer.writeheader(); writer.writerows(catches)
   110	    output={
   111	        "status":"PASS_WITH_CAVEATS","identity_rows":identity_rows,"path_rows":path_count,"summary_rows":summary_count,
   112	        "endpoint_rows_compared":compared,"endpoint_mismatches":0,"unstable_stencils":unstable,
   113	        "max_projector_validation_residual":result["max_projector_validation_residual"],
   114	        "max_derivative_convergence_residual":result["max_derivative_convergence_residual"],
   115	        "independent_blind_path_comparisons":independent["blind_path_family_comparisons"],
   116	        "independent_adverse_path_comparisons":independent["adverse_path_family_comparisons"],
   117	        "catch_proofs":len(catches),"maximum_conclusion":"BOUNDED_METRIC_MOTIF_TO_HOPF_CORRESPONDENCE_CHARACTERIZED",
   118	    }
   119	    (HERE/"VERIFICATION_RESULT.json").write_text(json.dumps(output,indent=2,sort_keys=True)+"\n",encoding="utf-8")
   120	    print(json.dumps(output,indent=2,sort_keys=True))

The first package-contract replay caught a readout-only ordering error in its expected text string

## Independent verification

An independent verifier imports neither the production core nor builder. It independently rebuilt
metric curvature, scalar Hessian, all five instrument groups, generated algebras, commutants,
centers, real-primary projectors, block signatures, gradient incidence, Ricci/Hessian alignment,
edge relations, and both nonlinear chart transformations.

The anchor set was frozen by configuration-ID hash before saved classifications were read. On 384
configurations it reproduced 11,904 original and 23,808 transformed classifications—35,712 saved
comparisons—with zero discordance. Its worst saved-projector distance was
`5.223932397768749e-12`; its worst nonlinear covariance residual was
`1.9608027118610747e-16`. Omitting the nonlinear scalar-Hessian jet term produced the required
nonzero catch residual `0.012773925363472115`.

The first independent K09 implementation compared a valid alternate linear chart with the same
pointwise Jacobian; the complete tensor transformation correctly gave zero rather than exposing an
omitted nonlinear jet. That failed transcript is preserved. The corrected K09 keeps the transformed
metric jets but deliberately omits the scalar-Hessian chain-rule term proportional to the inverse-map
second jet, producing the nonzero residual above. `VERIFIER_IMPLEMENTATION_CORRECTION.md` records the
correction; no atlas outcome or tolerance was changed.

Because the blind anchors happened to include no uncertain original classifications, a separately
preregistered post-outcome escalation targeted **every** unique identity in the complete 162-row
margin ledger. It independently replayed 124 unique original identities and 248 transformed
identities. It retained 156 uncertain classifications and found zero discordant identities. No row
was selected by scientific appearance.

All 12 production catches and 12 independent catches pass. `VERIFICATION_RESULT.json` and
`MARGIN_ESCALATION_RESULT.json` are machine-readable records.

Before final replay, an internal audit found that the edge and operator-count mutation catches used

def validate_registry(registry):
    if len(registry) != 31 or [int(row["mask"]) for row in registry] != list(range(1, 32)): raise AssertionError("subset registry")
    for row in registry:
        keys = tuple(row["operator_keys"].split(";")); mask = sum(BITS[key] for key in keys)
        if mask != int(row["mask"]): raise AssertionError("registry key/mask")

codex
A more consequential provenance issue is now confirmed: the production builder directly imports the amplitude-volume family and joint invariant-subspace core, but neither appears in this package’s frozen-source hash table. The blind verifier independently reconstructs the analytic family and replays all adverse paths, which mitigates outcome corruption, but it does not make the stated “all frozen sources” gate literally true. I’m checking whether those hashes are transitively pinned by the frozen parent manifests.

import sympy as s
p=s.symbols('p', real=True)
A=s.Function('A')(p); O=s.Function('O')(p)
g=s.diag(-1,A**2,O**2*s.exp(-2*p),O**2*s.exp(2*p)); gi=s.simplify(g.inv())
coords=(s.symbols('t'),p,s.symbols('x1'),s.symbols('x2')); n=4
G=[[[s.simplify(sum(gi[i,l]*(s.diff(g[l,k],coords[j])+s.diff(g[l,j],coords[k])-s.diff(g[j,k],coords[l])) for l in range(n))/2) for k in range(n)] for j in range(n)] for i in range(n)]
# H"'^i_j = g''^{ia} nabla_a nabla_j p = -g''^{ia} Gamma''^p_{aj}
H=s.Matrix(n,n,lambda i,j:s.simplify(-sum(gi[i,a]*G[1][a][j] for a in range(n))))
D=s.zeros(n); D[1,1]=s.simplify(gi[1,1])
K=s.Matrix([0,0,1,1]); Kflat=g*K; Kn=s.simplify((K.T*g*K)[0]); conn=[s.simplify(v/Kn) for v in Kflat]
f=conn[2]
print('"'H=',H)
print('D=',D)
print('angular_gap=',s.simplify(H[3,3]-H[2,2]))
print('diag_connection=',conn)
print('common_scale_derivative=',s.simplify(s.diff(f,O)))
print('f=',f,'fprime=',s.simplify(s.diff(f,p)))
# coefficient of A wedge dA in dp"'^dx1''^dx2
print('"'A_wedge_dA_coefficient=',s.simplify(s.diff(f,p)))
# exact standard Hopf map under tan(eta)=e"'^(2p)
eta=s.atan(s.exp(2*p)); delta=s.symbols('"'delta', real=True)
print('sin2eta-sech=',s.simplify(s.sin(2*eta)-s.sech(2*p)))
print('cos2eta+tanh=',s.simplify(s.cos(2*eta)+s.tanh(2*p)))

   212	def projector_digest(projectors) -> str:
   213	    values = [[[float(value) for value in row] for row in np.asarray(projector)] for projector in projectors]

   217	def covariant_projector_derivative(projector: np.ndarray, partial: np.ndarray, gamma: np.ndarray) -> np.ndarray:
   218	    result = np.asarray(partial, dtype=float).copy()
   219	    for rho, nu, beta, sigma in itertools.product(range(4), repeat=4):
   220	        result[rho, nu, beta] += (
   221	            gamma[nu, rho, sigma] * projector[sigma, beta]
   222	            - gamma[sigma, rho, beta] * projector[nu, sigma]
   223	        )
   224	    return result
   225	
   226	
   227	def frobenius_obstruction(projector: np.ndarray, partial: np.ndarray, gamma: np.ndarray) -> float:
   228	    nabla = covariant_projector_derivative(projector, partial, gamma)
   229	    term = np.zeros((4, 4, 4))
   230	    for nu, alpha, beta, rho in itertools.product(range(4), repeat=4):
   231	        term[nu, alpha, beta] += (
   232	            projector[rho, alpha] * nabla[rho, nu, beta]
   233	            - projector[rho, beta] * nabla[rho, nu, alpha]
   234	        )
   235	    complement = np.eye(4) - projector
   236	    obstruction = np.einsum("mn,nab->mab", complement, term)
   237	    return float(np.linalg.norm(obstruction) / max(np.linalg.norm(nabla), 1.0e-30))

    11	## Result first
    12	
    13	The new motif vocabulary does connect to the Hopf program, but at two sharply different levels.
    14	
    15	First, the complete registered local analytic ensemble contains abundant coherent projector bundles
    16	and genuine anholonomy. Of 95,232 instrument-family paths, 93,920 retain one stable projector motif
    17	through all 17 nodes. At the path midpoints, 8,205 families carry the `1+1+2` motif. Its primitive
    18	Lorentzian rank-two plane is locally nonintegrable in 6,669 cases and integrable in 1,536. The 1,395
    19	four-line midpoints have three complementary rank-two splittings; all 8,370 tested split sides are
    20	locally nonintegrable. Thus the metric instruments commonly supply twisting planes rather than only
    21	stacked coordinate surfaces.
    22	
    23	Second, in the already conditional reciprocal-toric class,
    24	
    25	```text
    26	g = -dt^2 + A(phi)^2 dphi^2
    27	    + Omega(phi)^2[exp(-2phi) dxi1^2 + exp(2phi) dxi2^2],
    28	```
    29	
    30	the metric `phi` Hessian plus the unnormalized gradient dyad generically recovers the four intrinsic
    31	axes `(t,phi,xi1,xi2)` without an `S2` carrier. The two angular Hessian eigenvalues differ exactly by
    32	`2/A^2`; the dyad distinguishes depth from time. Axis recovery fails only at disclosed degeneracies
    33	`Omega'/Omega=+/-1` unless another intrinsic instrument resolves them.
    34	
    35	Once periodic circles, a free diagonal/anti-diagonal action, full reciprocal range, and opposite
    36	primitive caps are separately supplied, the metric-dual connection is independent of `Omega` and
    37	has conditional unit Hopf class. Its quotient map is exactly the same degree-one Hopf map used by
    38	the historical `hopf_seed` code after `tan(eta)=exp(2phi)`.
    39	
    40	This is the first direct vocabulary-to-Hopf bridge: metric instruments can provide local twisting
    41	projectors, and the reciprocal-toric specialization turns their angular axes into the exact Hopf
    42	seed geometry. It is a geometric precursor and compatibility witness, not native carrier or matter
    43	emergence.
    44

    73	complete transition census is `FAMILY_TRANSITION_CENSUS.tsv`.
    74	
    75	The endpoints reproduce all 190,464 corresponding rows of the frozen pointwise motif atlas with
    76	zero classification disagreement.
    77	
    78	These paths are coherent analytic configurations, not EOM solutions or physical evolution. They
    79	are open paths, so they establish continuation and endpoint permutation transport, not holonomy.
    80	
    81	## Local distributions
    82	
    83	Every midpoint received complete `h=1e-4` and `h/2` four-coordinate stencils. The largest derivative
    84	convergence residual is `0.0031622520541422948`, below the preregistered `0.005` gate. Only 13
    85	identity/family stencils are retained as degenerate or numerically uncertain; independent replay
    86	reproduces all 13.
    87	
    88	The main distribution observations are:
    89	
    90	- `1+1+2`: 6,669 primitive Lorentzian planes locally nonintegrable; 1,536 integrable.
    91	- Four lines: 8,370 complementary rank-two split sides locally nonintegrable; zero integrable.
    92	- `1+3`: 2,879 rank-three complements locally integrable and one uncertain. This agrees with the
    93	  hypersurface-orthogonal character expected of the nonzero `phi`-gradient dyad and reinforces that
    94	  the gradient alone is not a generic Hopf carrier.
    95	- Rank-one distributions are locally integrable by dimension, but remain unoriented lines.
    96	
    97	Nonintegrability is local twist/anholonomy. It is not a Hopf integer. No local family was assigned a
    98	compact domain, periodicity, cap, orientation lift, or global transition cocycle; therefore all
    99	3,072 receive `GLOBAL_DATA_ABSENT`, not `Q=0`.
   100	
   101	## Reciprocal-toric control
   102	
   103	For the conditional toric metric, the mixed Hessian and dyad eigenvalue pairs in the coordinate
   104	order `(t,phi,xi1,xi2)` are
   105	
   120	With the equal-weight diagonal generator separately supplied, the metric-dual connection is
   121	
   122	```text
   123	calA = f(phi) dxi1 + [1-f(phi)] dxi2,
   124	f(phi)=1/[1+exp(4phi)].
   125	```
   126	
   127	`Omega` cancels. For finite endpoints,
   128	
   129	```text
   130	Q = f(phi_minus)-f(phi_plus),
   131	```
   132	
   133	so the readout is continuous and boundary-dependent, not automatically integral. Only the full
   134	range `phi: -infinity -> +infinity`, two `2*pi` circles, opposite primitive smooth collapses,
   135	selected free diagonal/anti-diagonal action, orientation, and normalization give `|Q|=1`.
   136	
   137	At `phi=0` the circle fractions are equal. Reciprocal reflection exchanges the two angular
   138	coefficients; it is a metric isometry only when `A^2` and `Omega^2` are even and the global circle
   139	exchange is supplied. The round control has exact opposite collapse limits `(1,0)` and `(0,1)`.
   140	Arbitrary positive `A,Omega` do not inherit periodicity or cap regularity from the local projectors.

   153	
   154	```text
   155	(sin(2eta) cos(delta), sin(2eta) sin(delta), cos(2eta)),
   156	```
   157	
   158	the degree-one Hopf map implemented by `hopf_seed` following inverse stereographic

codex
# Verdict: FAIL

The package’s `COMPLETE_VERIFIED_WITH_CAVEATS` grade and four “YES” evidence gates are not justified. This does not refute the underlying conditional toric/Hopf algebra; it fails the package’s verification claim.

## Blocking findings

1. **A preregistered covariance gate was never exercised.** The contract requires projector matching under coordinate transformations ([PREREGISTRATION.md](/tmp/udt_motif_hopf_20260722_zpmwYU/repo/udt_motif_hopf_correspondence_audit_2026-07-22/PREREGISTRATION.md:164)). Neither current verifier transforms the path projectors or their derivatives. Moreover, Frobenius and convergence thresholds use Euclidean component norms ([build_correspondence_atlas.py](/tmp/udt_motif_hopf_20260722_zpmwYU/repo/udt_motif_hopf_correspondence_audit_2026-07-22/build_correspondence_atlas.py:227)), which are chart-dependent. The Frobenius tensor formula itself is valid, but its numerical certification is only for the registered chart.

2. **The claimed independent toric verification is circular.** Production hard-codes the Hessian eigentuples and a standard Hopf map ([derive_toric_control.py](/tmp/udt_motif_hopf_20260722_zpmwYU/repo/udt_motif_hopf_correspondence_audit_2026-07-22/derive_toric_control.py:31)); the independent verifier hard-codes the same formulas rather than deriving them from the metric ([verify_correspondence_independent.py](/tmp/udt_motif_hopf_20260722_zpmwYU/repo/udt_motif_hopf_correspondence_audit_2026-07-22/verify_correspondence_independent.py:283)). The production script hashes `fs_hopfion.py` but never reads or compares its `hopf_seed` implementation. Therefore the report’s “exact independent toric” statement ([AUDIT_REPORT.md](/tmp/udt_motif_hopf_20260722_zpmwYU/repo/udt_motif_hopf_correspondence_audit_2026-07-22/AUDIT_REPORT.md:185)) is unsupported by its packaged verifier.

3. **The catch proofs are largely assertions about declared fields, not mutation tests.** Several independent catches are tautologies such as `len(ids[:-1]) != 64`; package catches directly throw an `AssertionError` rather than pass corrupted evidence through the validator ([verify_package.py](/tmp/udt_motif_hopf_20260722_zpmwYU/repo/udt_motif_hopf_correspondence_audit_2026-07-22/verify_package.py:84)). Thus “11/11” and “13/13 catches” overstates validator strength.

4. **Carrier/action accounting is internally contradictory.** The connection and quotient use a supplied equal-weight diagonal action, yet the result records `construction_used_carrier_or_action: false` ([derive_toric_control.py](/tmp/udt_motif_hopf_20260722_zpmwYU/repo/udt_motif_hopf_correspondence_audit_2026-07-22/derive_toric_control.py:90)). The package verifier enforces that false boolean while separately requiring the action-premise string. The report’s prose correctly calls the action supplied, but the machine catch does not audit import.

5. **“Coherent projector bundles” exceeds the sampled evidence.** Stability means equal motif at 17 nodes with matchable labels; it has no continuity-distance gate ([build_correspondence_atlas.py](/tmp/udt_motif_hopf_20260722_zpmwYU/repo/udt_motif_hopf_correspondence_audit_2026-07-22/build_correspondence_atlas.py:418)). Among paths labelled stable, 70 have maximum adjacent component distance above `0.5`, 33 above `1`, and the maximum is `6.57`. A 257-node replay of the worst path retained its motif, so this is not a found counterexample, but the evidence supports sampled continuation—not a continuous bundle theorem or independently verified endpoint transport.

## Checks that did pass

- Both requested verifiers completed and reproduced their banked `PASS_WITH_CAVEATS` outputs byte-for-byte. They were run in a temporary mirror because they write result files; I made no worktree edits.
- All declared frozen manifests and their contents passed SHA-256 checks, including the transitively pinned amplitude-volume and joint-invariant sources.
- All path, summary, and distribution primary keys are unique. Threshold labels match their stored values.
- The Frobenius projector formula has the correct tensor index structure. Nonintegrable rows are well separated in the registered chart: minimum `9.73e-4` versus the `1e-5` gate. Integrable maximum is `5.16e-8`; one row remains uncertain.
- The `8,370` four-line rows are six distinct rank-two planes per midpoint, not duplicate keys. However, the `1+1+2` atlas semantically repeats its primitive rank-two plane as one complementary-split side—8,205 extra diagnostic rows.
